id="Accordion-item-0" role="region" tabindex="-1"><div class="BioAbout l-row"><div class="BioAbout-content l-col-xs-12 l-col-sm-10 l-col-md-8-up"><h4 class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--title">About Me</h4><div class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--main">Joe is a Senior Vice President, Portfolio Management Director, and Senior Member of The Bridge Group at Morgan Stanleys Northfield, NJ branch office.  He holds the designation of Certified Portfolio Manager (CPM).  Joe has had the good fortune to work with families who desire goals based solutions for wealth and investment planning.  My investing process is based on a client centric approach, with close attention paid to risk tolerance and the time horizon for achievement.  Each relationship is unique with a tailored plan of action.  I draw on professional experience, training, research and the vast resources of Morgan Stanley.<br/><br/>On November 2, 1991, Joe began is Financial Services career at Dean Witter Reynolds, Inc.  At the time, we were part of the Sears Financial Network.  Needless to say, the world has changed dramatically, and Joe has been a advisor to many valued clients and families.  Through spinoffs and mergers, Dean Witter became Morgan Stanley. On January 1, 2000 the Diamond Enstice Dugan Group was formed.  Nat Diamond and Tom Enstice have since retired, and Joe is grateful to have worked alongside both men who accomplished so much for clients during their careers.  In July of 2017, Ryan Leek joined Morgan Stanley and The Bridge Group was formed.<br/><br/>Joe graduated from St. Louis University in 1986 with a Bachelors of Science in Finance from the business school.  He lives in Linwood, NJ with Enita and their son, Colin.  For enjoyment, Joe enjoys swimming, functional fitness training, golf, and snow skiing (especially with Colin).  Joe volunteers his time to his Church (Our Lady of Sorrows) and is committed to charitable efforts of the Catholic Church and finding a cure for melanoma.</div><div class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--small">Securities Agent: MA, MI, MN, MO, NC, NJ, NY, OK, OR, PA, RI, SC, TN, TX, VA, WI, MD, AZ, CA, CO, CT, DC, DE, FL, GA, IL, IN, LA; General Securities Representative; Investment Advisor Representative; Managed Futures<br/>NMLS#: 1412078</div></div></div></div><div aria-live="polite" class="js-accordion-item Accordion-item" data-accordion-index="1" id="Accordion-item-1" role="region" tabindex="-1"><div class="BioAbout l-row"><div class="BioAbout-content l-col-xs-12 l-col-sm-10 l-col-md-8-up"><h4 class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--title">About Me</h4><div class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--main">Ryan Leek is a Financial Advisor in Morgan Stanleys Northfield, NJ office.  He works with a select group of families, business owners, and individuals to build and protect wealth over multiple generations. Ryan draws on the global investment resources of Morgan Stanley as well as his professional experience to deliver a tailored, client centric approach to planning and investing.<br/><br/>Prior to joining Morgan Stanley, Ryan spent 5 years at J.P.Morgan Chase &amp; Co.  Most recently, he spent 2 years as a Private Banking Analyst in J.P. Morgans Center City Philadelphia office, supporting ultra-high net worth families and individuals in the Mid-Atlantic Region with their wealth management affairs.  Before this, Ryan spent a year and a half as a Capacity &amp; Planning Associate, and two years in J.P. Morgans Corporate Analyst Development Program, a cross line of business leadership program focused on Metrics and Analytics, Process Improvement,  Project Management, and Operational Risk &amp; Controls.<br/><br/>In his spare time, Ryan enjoys the thrill of the outdoors. In the winter, he can be found at Camelback Ski Area in the Poconos, coaching youth athletes in the Pocono Alpine Ski Education Foundation. In the summer, he can be found in Cape May, NJ participating in various offshore fishing events.<br/><br/>Ryan is a graduate of the Martin J. Whitman School of Management at Syracuse University 12, with a B.S. in Finance and Entrepreneurship &amp; Emerging Enterprises. During his time at Syracuse University, he was a member of the Syracuse University Alpine Ski Team and was named to the USCSA Academic All-American Team in three of four competitive seasons.<br/><br/>Investments and services offered through Morgan Stanley Smith Barney LLC.  Member SIPC.<br/>CRC 2527290 5/19</div><div class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--small">Securities Agent: MA, OK, TN, WI, VA, TX, SC, RI, PA, NY, NJ, NC, MO, MN, MI, MD, LA, IN, IL, GA, FL, DE, DC, CT, CO, CA, AZ; General Securities Representative; Investment Advisor Representative<br/>NMLS#: 1843720</div></div></div></div><div aria-live="polite" class="js-accordion-item Accordion-item" data-accordion-index="2" id="Accordion-item-2" role="region" tabindex="-1"><div class="BioAbout l-row"><div class="BioAbout-content l-col-xs-12 l-col-sm-10 l-col-md-8-up"><h4 class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--title">About Me</h4><div class="BioAbout-row BioAbout-row--main">Debra Costanzo Cline is a senior client service associate for Morgan Stanley and The Bridge Group.  Deb is a native of Southern NJ, after attending Rowan University, she entered the world of financial services.   Deb joined The Bridge Group in March of 2019; she boasts more than three decades in the financial services industry. Her main focus is providing comprehensive service to our clients and our team members while serving as our primary point of contact for all aspects of administration and daily operations. She enjoys the challenges of being on the operations front line when helping our clients achieve their goals While utilizing her years of industry experience, she has held positions that include operations management for several major financial services firms while maintaining her Series 7 and 63 licenses.  <br/><br/>        In her personal life, she pursues two main passions, horses and traveling. She and her husband, Jerry, own a small horse farm, which offers them the opportunity to enjoy a traveling equine lifestyle.
